## License: unknown

.js
import React from 'react';

import './index.css';
import App from './App';

const root = ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById('root'));
root.render(
  <React.StrictMode>
    <App />
  </React.StrictMode>
);
``
```

## License: unknown

  <React.StrictMode>
    <App />
  </React.StrictMode>
);
``
```

  const [error, setError] = useState(null);

  const handleChange = (e) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    setFormData({
      ...formData,
      [name]: value
    });
  };

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault
```
